## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Ceph OSD Authentication and Cephx Protocol Implementation

## Your Task

Find all C++ source and header files in ceph/ceph under src/auth/ and src/mon/ that implement the Cephx authentication protocol used by OSD daemons. Identify: the CephxServiceHandler and CephxClientHandler classes, the AuthAuthorizer interface, the MonClient authentication handshake methods, the key rotation and ticket generation logic, and any files defining the AUTH_CEPHX protocol message types. Report each file path and the primary class or struct it defines.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/ceph--v19.2.1.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

68-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully identified and documented all the C++ files implementing the Cephx authentication protocol in Ceph. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings:

**Core Cephx Implementation Files (src/auth/cephx/):**
- **CephxClientHandler** - Client-side authentication handler
- **CephxServiceHandler** - Service-side handler for OSD/MDS authentication
- **CephxAuthorizeHandler** - Implements authorization verification for connections
- **CephxKeyServer** - Central key management with ticket generation and key rotation
- **CephxSessionHandler** - Per-session cryptographic operations
- **CephxProtocol.h** - Protocol message structures

**Protocol Message Structures:**
- CephXAuthorizer, CephXTicketHandler, CephXTicketManager
- CephXServiceTicket, CephXAuthenticate, CephXServerChallenge
- CephXAuthorizeChallenge, CephXAuthorizeReply

**Base Authentication Classes:**
- AuthAuthorizer interface and its implementations
- AuthServiceHandler, AuthClientHandler, AuthSessionHandler
- RotatingSecrets and ExpiringCryptoKey for key rotation
- RotatingKeyRing for managing rotating keys

**Monitor-Side Authentication:**
- AuthMonitor for managing authentication state
- MonClient and MonConnection for client-monitor authentication handshakes
- MAuth and MAuthReply protocol messages

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file listings, symbols, and detailed narrative explanation of the Cephx implementation architecture.
